Queen's Doughnuts is a family owned business that has been a regular stop of the driver's of the highly travelled Durfee Avenue as well as the local residents in southern El Monte. This shop features everything from your typical doughnut selection, hot sandwiches to an extensive array of boba drinks and also "Thrifty" brand Ice Cream for a cold treat. There are a number of other cold bottled beverages available as well as snacks like potato chips to boot.<//text>

< review>
As someone who buys a lot of products from Drop (since 2018) I can say that one has to be very careful when buying from them. While they do offer some very good deals every once in a while, you have to research before pulling the trigger. Their delivery times vary wildly (from a few days for in-stock products to sometimes more than a year for group buys), their return/refund policy is unclear and will vary on a case-by-case basis (they tend to be better with their own "Drop Studio" products), and sometimes you can simply find the same product cheaper and delivered quicker elsewhere. So, do your homework before buying from them! This is not a store for impulse buys.<//review>

They stated that the real problem was the crank shaft and the bearings- the mechanic said this is the second time it's happened to him in his life  and is very unusual - MAYBE because you made a mistake and improperly diagnosed the problem?? I am still in the process of resolving this matter, however the mechanics will not admit ANY fault.  I highly suggest you take your vehicle to another automotive shop - or have it towed somewhere else to have the work done.<//review>
